290 //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===// ----
291 // ----
292 // Mips Asm Directives ----
293 // ----
294 // -- Frame directive "frame Stackpointer, Stacksize, RARegister" ----
295 // Describe the stack frame. ----
296 // ----
297 // -- Mask directives "(f)mask bitmask, offset" ----
298 // Tells the assembler which registers are saved and where. ----
299 // bitmask - contain a little endian bitset indicating which registers are ----
300 // saved on function prologue (e.g. with a 0x80000000 mask, the ----
301 // assembler knows the register 31 (RA) is saved at prologue. ----
302 // offset - the position before stack pointer subtraction indicating where ----
303 // the first saved register on prologue is located. (e.g. with a ----
304 // ----
305 // Consider the following function prologue: ----
306 // ----
307 // .frame $fp,48,$ra ----
308 // .mask 0xc0000000,-8 ----
309 // addiu $sp, $sp, -48 ----
310 // sw $ra, 40($sp) ----
311 // sw $fp, 36($sp) ----
312 // ----
313 // With a 0xc0000000 mask, the assembler knows the register 31 (RA) and ----
314 // 30 (FP) are saved at prologue. As the save order on prologue is from ----
315 // left to right, RA is saved first. A -8 offset means that after the ----
316 // stack pointer subtration, the first register in the mask (RA) will be ----
317 // saved at address 48-8=40. ----
318 // ----
319 //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===// ----
320 ----
321 //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===// ----
322 // Mask directives ----
323 //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===// ----
324 ----
325 // Create a bitmask with all callee saved registers for CPU or Floating Point ----
326 // registers. For CPU registers consider RA, GP and FP for saving if necessary. ----

328 // CPU and FPU Saved Registers Bitmasks ----

331 ----

357 CPUBitmask |= (1 << RegNum); 4 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
358 } ----
359 ----

361 FPUTopSavedRegOff = FPUBitmask ? 2 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll

363 ----
364 // CPU Regs are saved below FP Regs. ----
365 CPUTopSavedRegOff = CPUBitmask ? -CSFPRegsSize - CPURegSize : 0; 2 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
366 ----
367 MipsTargetStreamer &TS = getTargetStreamer(); 2 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll

474 /// isBlockOnlyReachableByFallthough - Return true if the basic block has ----
475 /// exactly one predecessor and the control transfer mechanism between ----
476 /// the predecessor and this block is a fall-through. ----
477 bool MipsAsmPrinter::isBlockOnlyReachableByFallthrough(const MachineBasicBlock* 8 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
478 MBB) const { ----
479 // The predecessor has to be immediately before this block. ----
480 const MachineBasicBlock *Pred = *MBB->pred_begin(); 8 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
481 ----
482 // If the predecessor is a switch statement, assume a jump table ----
483 // implementation, so it is not a fall through. ----
484 if (const BasicBlock *bb = Pred->getBasicBlock()) 8 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
485 if (isa(bb->getTerminator())) 8 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
486 return false; 0
487 ----
488 // If this is a landing pad, it isn't a fall through. If it has no preds, ----
489 // then nothing falls through to it. ----
490 if (MBB->isEHPad() || MBB->pred_empty()) 8 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
491 return false; 0
492 ----
493 // If there isn't exactly one predecessor, it can't be a fall through. ----
494 MachineBasicBlock::const_pred_iterator PI = MBB->pred_begin(), PI2 = PI; 8 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
495 ++PI2; 8 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
496 ----
497 if (PI2 != MBB->pred_end()) 8 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
498 return false; 2 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
499 ----
500 // The predecessor has to be immediately before this block. ----
501 if (!Pred->isLayoutSuccessor(MBB)) 6 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
502 return false; 2 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
503 ----
504 // If the block is completely empty, then it definitely does fall through. ----
505 if (Pred->empty()) 4 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
506 return true; 0
507 ----
508 // Otherwise, check the last instruction. ----
509 // Check if the last terminator is an unconditional branch. ----
510 MachineBasicBlock::const_iterator I = Pred->end(); 4 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
511 while (I != Pred->begin() && !(--I)->isTerminator()) ; 4 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
512 ----
513 return !I->isBarrier(); 4 ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips_dbg.ll ../DebugInfoTest/example_mips.ll
514 } ----

516 // Print out an operand for an inline asm expression. ----
517 bool MipsAsmPrinter::PrintAsmOperand(const MachineInstr *MI, unsigned OpNum, 0
518 const char *ExtraCode, raw_ostream &O) { ----
519 // Does this asm operand have a single letter operand modifier? ----
520 if (ExtraCode && ExtraCode[0]) { 0
521 if (ExtraCode[1] != 0) return true; // Unknown modifier. 0
522 ----
523 const MachineOperand &MO = MI->getOperand(OpNum); 0
524 switch (ExtraCode[0]) { 0
525 default: 0
526 // See if this is a generic print operand ----
527 return AsmPrinter::PrintAsmOperand(MI, OpNum, ExtraCode, O); 0
528 case 'X': // hex const int 0
529 if (!MO.isImm()) 0
530 return true; 0
531 O << "0x" << Twine::utohexstr(MO.getImm()); 0
532 return false; 0
533 case 'x': // hex const int (low 16 bits) 0
534 if (!MO.isImm()) 0
535 return true; 0
536 O << "0x" << Twine::utohexstr(MO.getImm() & 0xffff); 0
537 return false; 0
538 case 'd': // decimal const int 0
539 if (!MO.isImm()) 0
540 return true; 0
541 O << MO.getImm(); 0
542 return false; 0
543 case 'm': // decimal const int minus 1 0
544 if (!MO.isImm()) 0
545 return true; 0
546 O << MO.getImm() - 1; 0
547 return false; 0
548 case 'y': // exact log2 0
549 if (!MO.isImm()) 0
550 return true; 0
551 if (!isPowerOf2_64(MO.getImm())) 0
552 return true; 0
553 O << Log2_64(MO.getImm()); 0
554 return false; 0
555 case 'z': 0
556 // $0 if zero, regular printing otherwise ----
557 if (MO.isImm() && MO.getImm() == 0) { 0
558 O << "$0"; 0
559 return false; 0
560 } ----
561 // If not, call printOperand as normal. ----
562 break; 0
563 case 'D': // Second part of a double word register operand 0
564 case 'L': // Low order register of a double word register operand ----
565 case 'M': // High order register of a double word register operand ----
566 { ----
567 if (OpNum == 0) 0
568 return true; 0
569 const MachineOperand &FlagsOP = MI->getOperand(OpNum - 1); 0
570 if (!FlagsOP.isImm()) 0
571 return true; 0
572 unsigned Flags = FlagsOP.getImm(); 0
573 unsigned NumVals = InlineAsm::getNumOperandRegisters(Flags); 0
574 // Number of registers represented by this operand. We are looking ----
575 // for 2 for 32 bit mode and 1 for 64 bit mode. ----
576 if (NumVals != 2) { 0
577 if (Subtarget->isGP64bit() && NumVals == 1 && MO.isReg()) { 0
578 Register Reg = MO.getReg(); 0
579 O << '$' << MipsInstPrinter::getRegisterName(Reg); 0
580 return false; 0
581 } ----
582 return true; 0
583 } ----
584 ----
585 unsigned RegOp = OpNum; 0
586 if (!Subtarget->isGP64bit()){ 0
587 // Endianness reverses which register holds the high or low value ----
588 // between M and L. ----
589 switch(ExtraCode[0]) { 0
590 case 'M': 0
591 RegOp = (Subtarget->isLittle()) ? OpNum + 1 : OpNum; 0
592 break; 0
593 case 'L': 0
594 RegOp = (Subtarget->isLittle()) ? OpNum : OpNum + 1; 0
595 break; 0
596 case 'D': // Always the second part 0
597 RegOp = OpNum + 1; 0
598 } ----
599 if (RegOp >= MI->getNumOperands()) 0
600 return true; 0
601 const MachineOperand &MO = MI->getOperand(RegOp); 0
602 if (!MO.isReg()) 0
603 return true; 0
604 Register Reg = MO.getReg(); 0
605 O << '$' << MipsInstPrinter::getRegisterName(Reg); 0
606 return false; 0
607 } ----
608 break; 0
609 } ----
610 case 'w': 0
611 // Print MSA registers for the 'f' constraint ----
612 // In LLVM, the 'w' modifier doesn't need to do anything. ----
613 // We can just call printOperand as normal. ----
614 break; 0
615 } ----
616 } ----
617 ----
618 printOperand(MI, OpNum, O); 0
619 return false; 0
620 } ----

622 bool MipsAsmPrinter::PrintAsmMemoryOperand(const MachineInstr *MI, 0
623 unsigned OpNum, ----
624 const char *ExtraCode, ----
625 raw_ostream &O) { ----
626 assert(OpNum + 1 < MI->getNumOperands() && "Insufficient operands"); 0
627 const MachineOperand &BaseMO = MI->getOperand(OpNum); 0
628 const MachineOperand &OffsetMO = MI->getOperand(OpNum + 1); 0
629 assert(BaseMO.isReg() && 0
630 "Unexpected base pointer for inline asm memory operand."); ----
631 assert(OffsetMO.isImm() && 0
632 "Unexpected offset for inline asm memory operand."); ----
633 int Offset = OffsetMO.getImm(); 0
634 ----
635 // Currently we are expecting either no ExtraCode or 'D','M','L'. ----
636 if (ExtraCode) { 0
637 switch (ExtraCode[0]) { 0
638 case 'D': 0
639 Offset += 4; 0
640 break; 0
641 case 'M': 0
642 if (Subtarget->isLittle()) 0
643 Offset += 4; 0
644 break; 0
645 case 'L': 0
646 if (!Subtarget->isLittle()) 0
647 Offset += 4; 0
648 break; 0
649 default: 0
650 return true; // Unknown modifier. 0
651 } ----
652 } ----
653 ----
654 O << Offset << "($" << MipsInstPrinter::getRegisterName(BaseMO.getReg()) 0
655 << ")"; 0
656 ----
657 return false; 0
658 } ----
659 ----
660 void MipsAsmPrinter::printOperand(const MachineInstr *MI, int opNum, 0
661 raw_ostream &O) { ----
662 const MachineOperand &MO = MI->getOperand(opNum); 0
663 bool closeP = false; 0
664 ----
665 if (MO.getTargetFlags()) 0
666 closeP = true; 0
667 ----
668 switch(MO.getTargetFlags()) { 0
669 case MipsII::MO_GPREL: O << "%gp_rel("; break; 0
670 case MipsII::MO_GOT_CALL: O << "%call16("; break; 0
671 case MipsII::MO_GOT: O << "%got("; break; 0
672 case MipsII::MO_ABS_HI: O << "%hi("; break; 0
673 case MipsII::MO_ABS_LO: O << "%lo("; break; 0
674 case MipsII::MO_HIGHER: O << "%higher("; break; 0
675 case MipsII::MO_HIGHEST: O << "%highest(("; break; 0
676 case MipsII::MO_TLSGD: O << "%tlsgd("; break; 0
677 case MipsII::MO_GOTTPREL: O << "%gottprel("; break; 0
678 case MipsII::MO_TPREL_HI: O << "%tprel_hi("; break; 0
679 case MipsII::MO_TPREL_LO: O << "%tprel_lo("; break; 0
680 case MipsII::MO_GPOFF_HI: O << "%hi(%neg(%gp_rel("; break; 0
681 case MipsII::MO_GPOFF_LO: O << "%lo(%neg(%gp_rel("; break; 0
682 case MipsII::MO_GOT_DISP: O << "%got_disp("; break; 0
683 case MipsII::MO_GOT_PAGE: O << "%got_page("; break; 0
684 case MipsII::MO_GOT_OFST: O << "%got_ofst("; break; 0
685 } ----
686 ----
687 switch (MO.getType()) { 0
688 case MachineOperand::MO_Register: 0
689 O << '$' 0
690 << StringRef(MipsInstPrinter::getRegisterName(MO.getReg())).lower(); 0
691 break; 0
692 ----
693 case MachineOperand::MO_Immediate: 0
694 O << MO.getImm(); 0
695 break; 0
696 ----
697 case MachineOperand::MO_MachineBasicBlock: 0
698 MO.getMBB()->getSymbol()->print(O, MAI); 0
699 return; 0
700 ----
701 case MachineOperand::MO_GlobalAddress: 0
702 PrintSymbolOperand(MO, O); 0
703 break; 0
704 ----
705 case MachineOperand::MO_BlockAddress: { 0
706 MCSymbol *BA = GetBlockAddressSymbol(MO.getBlockAddress()); 0
707 O << BA->getName(); 0
708 break; 0
709 } ----
710 ----
711 case MachineOperand::MO_ConstantPoolIndex: 0
712 O << getDataLayout().getPrivateGlobalPrefix() << "CPI" 0
713 << getFunctionNumber() << "_" << MO.getIndex(); 0
714 if (MO.getOffset()) 0
715 O << "+" << MO.getOffset(); 0
716 break; 0
717 ----
718 default: 0
719 llvm_unreachable(""); 0
720 } ----
721 ----
722 if (closeP) O << ")"; 0
723 } ----

736 case Mips::SWM32_MM: 0
737 case Mips::LWM32_MM: ----

739 break; 0
740 } ----
741 ----
742 printOperand(MI, opNum+1, O); 0
743 O << "("; 0

745 O << ")"; 0
746 } 0

838 ----
839 void MipsAsmPrinter::emitInlineAsmStart() const { 0
840 MipsTargetStreamer &TS = getTargetStreamer(); 0
841 ----
842 // GCC's choice of assembler options for inline assembly code ('at', 'macro' ----
843 // and 'reorder') is different from LLVM's choice for generated code ('noat', ----
844 // 'nomacro' and 'noreorder'). ----
845 // In order to maintain compatibility with inline assembly code which depends ----
846 // on GCC's assembler options being used, we have to switch to those options ----
847 // for the duration of the inline assembly block and then switch back. ----
848 TS.emitDirectiveSetPush(); 0
849 TS.emitDirectiveSetAt(); 0
850 TS.emitDirectiveSetMacro(); 0
851 TS.emitDirectiveSetReorder(); 0
852 OutStreamer->addBlankLine(); 0
853 } 0

856 const MCSubtargetInfo *EndInfo) const { ----
857 OutStreamer->addBlankLine(); 0
858 getTargetStreamer().emitDirectiveSetPop(); 0
859 } 0

876 ----
877 void MipsAsmPrinter::EmitInstrRegReg(const MCSubtargetInfo &STI, 0
878 unsigned Opcode, unsigned Reg1, ----
879 unsigned Reg2) { ----
880 MCInst I; 0
881 // ----
882 // Because of the current td files for Mips32, the operands for MTC1 ----
883 // appear backwards from their normal assembly order. It's not a trivial ----
884 // change to fix this in the td file so we adjust for it here. ----
885 // ----
886 if (Opcode == Mips::MTC1) { 0
887 unsigned Temp = Reg1; 0
888 Reg1 = Reg2; 0
889 Reg2 = Temp; 0
890 } ----
891 I.setOpcode(Opcode); 0
892 I.addOperand(MCOperand::createReg(Reg1)); 0

921 void MipsAsmPrinter::EmitSwapFPIntParams(const MCSubtargetInfo &STI, 0
922 Mips16HardFloatInfo::FPParamVariant PV, ----
923 bool LE, bool ToFP) { ----
924 using namespace Mips16HardFloatInfo; ----
925 ----
926 unsigned MovOpc = ToFP ? Mips::MTC1 : Mips::MFC1; 0
927 switch (PV) { 0
928 case FSig: 0
929 EmitInstrRegReg(STI, MovOpc, Mips::A0, Mips::F12); 0
930 break; 0
931 case FFSig: 0
932 EmitMovFPIntPair(STI, MovOpc, Mips::A0, Mips::A1, Mips::F12, Mips::F14, LE); 0
933 break; 0
934 case FDSig: 0
935 EmitInstrRegReg(STI, MovOpc, Mips::A0, Mips::F12); 0
936 EmitMovFPIntPair(STI, MovOpc, Mips::A2, Mips::A3, Mips::F14, Mips::F15, LE); 0
937 break; 0
938 case DSig: 0
939 EmitMovFPIntPair(STI, MovOpc, Mips::A0, Mips::A1, Mips::F12, Mips::F13, LE); 0
940 break; 0
941 case DDSig: 0
942 EmitMovFPIntPair(STI, MovOpc, Mips::A0, Mips::A1, Mips::F12, Mips::F13, LE); 0
943 EmitMovFPIntPair(STI, MovOpc, Mips::A2, Mips::A3, Mips::F14, Mips::F15, LE); 0
944 break; 0
945 case DFSig: 0
946 EmitMovFPIntPair(STI, MovOpc, Mips::A0, Mips::A1, Mips::F12, Mips::F13, LE); 0
947 EmitInstrRegReg(STI, MovOpc, Mips::A2, Mips::F14); 0
948 break; 0
949 case NoSig: 0
950 return; 0
951 } ----
952 } ----
953 ----
954 void MipsAsmPrinter::EmitSwapFPIntRetval( 0
955 const MCSubtargetInfo &STI, Mips16HardFloatInfo::FPReturnVariant RV, ----
956 bool LE) { ----
957 using namespace Mips16HardFloatInfo; ----
958 ----
959 unsigned MovOpc = Mips::MFC1; 0
960 switch (RV) { 0
961 case FRet: 0
962 EmitInstrRegReg(STI, MovOpc, Mips::V0, Mips::F0); 0
963 break; 0
964 case DRet: 0
965 EmitMovFPIntPair(STI, MovOpc, Mips::V0, Mips::V1, Mips::F0, Mips::F1, LE); 0
966 break; 0
967 case CFRet: 0

969 break; 0
970 case CDRet: 0
971 EmitMovFPIntPair(STI, MovOpc, Mips::V0, Mips::V1, Mips::F0, Mips::F1, LE); 0
972 EmitMovFPIntPair(STI, MovOpc, Mips::A0, Mips::A1, Mips::F2, Mips::F3, LE); 0
973 break; 0
974 case NoFPRet: 0
975 break; 0
976 } ----
977 } 0
978 ----
979 void MipsAsmPrinter::EmitFPCallStub( 0
980 const char *Symbol, const Mips16HardFloatInfo::FuncSignature *Signature) { ----
981 using namespace Mips16HardFloatInfo; ----
982 ----
983 MCSymbol *MSymbol = OutContext.getOrCreateSymbol(StringRef(Symbol)); 0
984 bool LE = getDataLayout().isLittleEndian(); 0
985 // Construct a local MCSubtargetInfo here. ----
986 // This is because the MachineFunction won't exist (but have not yet been ----
987 // freed) and since we're at the global level we can use the default ----
988 // constructed subtarget. ----
989 std::unique_ptr STI(TM.getTarget().createMCSubtargetInfo( 0
990 TM.getTargetTriple().str(), TM.getTargetCPU(), 0
991 TM.getTargetFeatureString())); 0
992 ----
993 // ----
994 // .global xxxx ----
995 // ----
996 OutStreamer->emitSymbolAttribute(MSymbol, MCSA_Global); 0
997 const char *RetType; ----
998 // ----
999 // make the comment field identifying the return and parameter ----
1000 // types of the floating point stub ----
1001 // # Stub function to call rettype xxxx (params) ----
1002 // ----
1003 switch (Signature->RetSig) { 0
1004 case FRet: 0
1005 RetType = "float"; 0
1006 break; 0
1007 case DRet: 0
1008 RetType = "double"; 0
1009 break; 0
1010 case CFRet: 0
1011 RetType = "complex"; 0
1012 break; 0
1013 case CDRet: 0
1014 RetType = "double complex"; 0
1015 break; 0
1016 case NoFPRet: 0
1017 RetType = ""; 0
1018 break; 0
1019 } ----
1020 const char *Parms; ----
1021 switch (Signature->ParamSig) { 0
1022 case FSig: 0
1023 Parms = "float"; 0
1024 break; 0
1025 case FFSig: 0
1026 Parms = "float, float"; 0
1027 break; 0
1028 case FDSig: 0
1029 Parms = "float, double"; 0
1030 break; 0
1031 case DSig: 0
1032 Parms = "double"; 0
1033 break; 0
1034 case DDSig: 0
1035 Parms = "double, double"; 0
1036 break; 0
1037 case DFSig: 0
1038 Parms = "double, float"; 0
1039 break; 0
1040 case NoSig: 0
1041 Parms = ""; 0
1042 break; 0
1043 } ----
1044 OutStreamer->AddComment("\t# Stub function to call " + Twine(RetType) + " " + 0
1045 Twine(Symbol) + " (" + Twine(Parms) + ")"); 0
1046 // ----
1047 // probably not necessary but we save and restore the current section state ----
1048 // ----
1049 OutStreamer->pushSection(); 0
1050 // ----
1051 // .section mips16.call.fpxxxx,"ax",@progbits ----
1052 // ----
1053 MCSectionELF *M = OutContext.getELFSection( 0
1054 ".mips16.call.fp." + std::string(Symbol), ELF::SHT_PROGBITS, 0
1055 ELF::SHF_ALLOC | ELF::SHF_EXECINSTR); ----
1056 OutStreamer->switchSection(M, nullptr); 0
1057 // ----
1058 // .align 2 ----
1059 // ----
1060 OutStreamer->emitValueToAlignment(Align(4)); 0
1061 MipsTargetStreamer &TS = getTargetStreamer(); 0
1062 // ----
1063 // .set nomips16 ----
1064 // .set nomicromips ----
1065 // ----
1066 TS.emitDirectiveSetNoMips16(); 0
1067 TS.emitDirectiveSetNoMicroMips(); 0
1068 // ----
1069 // .ent __call_stub_fp_xxxx ----
1070 // .type __call_stub_fp_xxxx,@function ----
1071 // __call_stub_fp_xxxx: ----
1072 // ----
1073 std::string x = "__call_stub_fp_" + std::string(Symbol); 0
1074 MCSymbolELF *Stub = ----
1075 cast(OutContext.getOrCreateSymbol(StringRef(x))); 0
1076 TS.emitDirectiveEnt(*Stub); 0
1077 MCSymbol *MType = ----
1078 OutContext.getOrCreateSymbol("__call_stub_fp_" + Twine(Symbol)); 0
1079 OutStreamer->emitSymbolAttribute(MType, MCSA_ELF_TypeFunction); 0
1080 OutStreamer->emitLabel(Stub); 0
1081 ----
1082 // Only handle non-pic for now. ----
1083 assert(!isPositionIndependent() && 0
1084 "should not be here if we are compiling pic"); ----
1085 TS.emitDirectiveSetReorder(); 0
1086 // ----
1087 // We need to add a MipsMCExpr class to MCTargetDesc to fully implement ----
1088 // stubs without raw text but this current patch is for compiler generated ----
1089 // functions and they all return some value. ----
1090 // The calling sequence for non pic is different in that case and we need ----
1091 // to implement %lo and %hi in order to handle the case of no return value ----
1092 // See the corresponding method in Mips16HardFloat for details. ----
1093 // ----
1094 // mov the return address to S2. ----
1095 // we have no stack space to store it and we are about to make another call. ----
1096 // We need to make sure that the enclosing function knows to save S2 ----
1097 // This should have already been handled. ----
1098 // ----
1099 // Mov $18, $31 ----
1100 ----
1101 EmitInstrRegRegReg(*STI, Mips::OR, Mips::S2, Mips::RA, Mips::ZERO); 0
1102 ----
1103 EmitSwapFPIntParams(*STI, Signature->ParamSig, LE, true); 0
1104 ----
1105 // Jal xxxx ----
1106 // ----
1107 EmitJal(*STI, MSymbol); 0
1108 ----
1109 // fix return values ----
1110 EmitSwapFPIntRetval(*STI, Signature->RetSig, LE); 0
1111 // ----
1112 // do the return ----
1113 // if (Signature->RetSig == NoFPRet) ----
1114 // llvm_unreachable("should not be any stubs here with no return value"); ----
1115 // else ----
1116 EmitInstrReg(*STI, Mips::JR, Mips::S2); 0
1117 ----
1118 MCSymbol *Tmp = OutContext.createTempSymbol(); 0
1119 OutStreamer->emitLabel(Tmp); 0
1120 const MCSymbolRefExpr *E = MCSymbolRefExpr::create(Stub, OutContext); 0
1121 const MCSymbolRefExpr *T = MCSymbolRefExpr::create(Tmp, OutContext); 0
1122 const MCExpr *T_min_E = MCBinaryExpr::createSub(T, E, OutContext); 0
1123 OutStreamer->emitELFSize(Stub, T_min_E); 0
1124 TS.emitDirectiveEnd(x); 0
1125 OutStreamer->popSection(); 0
1126 } 0

1144 void MipsAsmPrinter::EmitSled(const MachineInstr &MI, SledKind Kind) { 0
1145 const uint8_t NoopsInSledCount = Subtarget->isGP64bit() ? 15 : 11; 0
1146 // For mips32 we want to emit the following pattern: ----
1147 // ----
1148 // .Lxray_sled_N: ----
1149 // ALIGN ----
1150 // B .tmpN ----
1151 // 11 NOP instructions (44 bytes) ----
1152 // ADDIU T9, T9, 52 ----
1153 // .tmpN ----
1154 // ----
1155 // We need the 44 bytes (11 instructions) because at runtime, we'd ----
1156 // be patching over the full 48 bytes (12 instructions) with the following ----
1157 // pattern: ----
1158 // ----
1159 // ADDIU SP, SP, -8 ----
1160 // NOP ----
1161 // SW RA, 4(SP) ----
1162 // SW T9, 0(SP) ----
1163 // LUI T9, %hi(__xray_FunctionEntry/Exit) ----
1164 // ORI T9, T9, %lo(__xray_FunctionEntry/Exit) ----
1165 // LUI T0, %hi(function_id) ----
1166 // JALR T9 ----
1167 // ORI T0, T0, %lo(function_id) ----
1168 // LW T9, 0(SP) ----
1169 // LW RA, 4(SP) ----
1170 // ADDIU SP, SP, 8 ----
1171 // ----
1172 // We add 52 bytes to t9 because we want to adjust the function pointer to ----
1173 // the actual start of function i.e. the address just after the noop sled. ----
1174 // We do this because gp displacement relocation is emitted at the start of ----
1175 // of the function i.e after the nop sled and to correctly calculate the ----
1176 // global offset table address, t9 must hold the address of the instruction ----
1177 // containing the gp displacement relocation. ----
1178 // FIXME: Is this correct for the static relocation model? ----
1179 // ----
1180 // For mips64 we want to emit the following pattern: ----
1181 // ----
1182 // .Lxray_sled_N: ----
1183 // ALIGN ----
1184 // B .tmpN ----
1185 // 15 NOP instructions (60 bytes) ----
1186 // .tmpN ----
1187 // ----
1188 // We need the 60 bytes (15 instructions) because at runtime, we'd ----
1189 // be patching over the full 64 bytes (16 instructions) with the following ----
1190 // pattern: ----
1191 // ----
1192 // DADDIU SP, SP, -16 ----
1193 // NOP ----
1194 // SD RA, 8(SP) ----
1195 // SD T9, 0(SP) ----
1196 // LUI T9, %highest(__xray_FunctionEntry/Exit) ----
1197 // ORI T9, T9, %higher(__xray_FunctionEntry/Exit) ----
1198 // DSLL T9, T9, 16 ----
1199 // ORI T9, T9, %hi(__xray_FunctionEntry/Exit) ----
1200 // DSLL T9, T9, 16 ----
1201 // ORI T9, T9, %lo(__xray_FunctionEntry/Exit) ----
1202 // LUI T0, %hi(function_id) ----
1203 // JALR T9 ----
1204 // ADDIU T0, T0, %lo(function_id) ----
1205 // LD T9, 0(SP) ----
1206 // LD RA, 8(SP) ----
1207 // DADDIU SP, SP, 16 ----
1208 // ----
1209 OutStreamer->emitCodeAlignment(Align(4), &getSubtargetInfo()); 0
1210 auto CurSled = OutContext.createTempSymbol("xray_sled_", true); 0
1211 OutStreamer->emitLabel(CurSled); 0
1212 auto Target = OutContext.createTempSymbol(); 0
1213 ----
1214 // Emit "B .tmpN" instruction, which jumps over the nop sled to the actual ----
1215 // start of function ----
1216 const MCExpr *TargetExpr = MCSymbolRefExpr::create( 0
1217 Target, MCSymbolRefExpr::VariantKind::VK_None, OutContext); ----
1218 EmitToStreamer(*OutStreamer, MCInstBuilder(Mips::BEQ) 0
1219 .addReg(Mips::ZERO) 0
1220 .addReg(Mips::ZERO) 0
1221 .addExpr(TargetExpr)); 0
1222 ----
1223 for (int8_t I = 0; I < NoopsInSledCount; I++) 0
1224 EmitToStreamer(*OutStreamer, MCInstBuilder(Mips::SLL) 0
1225 .addReg(Mips::ZERO) 0
1226 .addReg(Mips::ZERO) 0
1227 .addImm(0)); 0
1228 ----
1229 OutStreamer->emitLabel(Target); 0
1230 ----
1231 if (!Subtarget->isGP64bit()) { 0
1232 EmitToStreamer(*OutStreamer, 0
1233 MCInstBuilder(Mips::ADDiu) 0
1234 .addReg(Mips::T9) 0
1235 .addReg(Mips::T9) 0
1236 .addImm(0x34)); 0
1237 } ----
1238 ----
1239 recordSled(CurSled, MI, Kind, 2); 0
1240 } 0

1282 void MipsAsmPrinter::NaClAlignIndirectJumpTargets(MachineFunction &MF) { 0

1291 } ----
1292 } ----
1293 ----

1295 for (auto &MBB : MF) { 0
1296 if (MBB.hasAddressTaken()) 0
1297 MBB.setAlignment(MIPS_NACL_BUNDLE_ALIGN); 0
